There is a smell of French perfume as soon as you enter the elevator. The lobby is luxurious and feels like a five-star hotel. The room is large, the bed is very comfortable, it has heating and a big bathtub. The hotel should have upgraded it for me. At the end of the 36th floor (probably the executive floor), the L-shaped room has two sides of floor-to-ceiling glass windows, with very good lighting and views! ! !
The breakfast is very rich and the children like it very much. It is a good deal if it includes breakfast. But if you have to pay 174 yuan/person, it is still too expensive and not worth it.
The hotel's facilities are very complete, the swimming pool and children's play area are very good! !
Although the location is a bit far from the scenic spots (Xiaoshan District used to be a suburb), it is very convenient to have a subway nearby. Although this hotel is further away, in terms of cost performance and overall standards, I think it is worth the distance! !
